/**
 * @copyright Zoom 2020
 * @namespace LanguageResource
 * @version WebSDK1.7.8
*/


/** Zoom office supported languages, en-US is default
 * @typedef languages
 * @method languages
 * @property {string} en-US - English default
 * @property {string} de-DE - German Deutsch
 * @property {string} es-ES - Spanish Español
 * @property {string} fr-FR - French Français
 * @property {string} jp-JP - Japanese 日本語
 * @property {string} pt-PT - Portuguese Portuguese
 * @property {string} ru-RU - Russian Русский
 * @property {string} zh-CN - Chinese 简体中文
 * @property {string} zh-TW - Chinese 繁体中文
 * @property {string} ko-KO - Korean 한국어
 */

const LanguageResource = {
  'en-US': 'English Default',
  'de-DE': 'German Deutsch',
  'es-ES': 'Spanish Español',
  'fr-FR': 'French Français',
  'jp-JP': 'Japanese 日本語',
  'pt-PT': 'Portuguese Portuguese',
  'ru-RU': 'Russian Русский',
  'zh-CN': 'Chinese 简体中文',
  'zh-TW': 'Chinese 繁体中文',
  'ko-KO': 'Korean 한국어',
};
